Код на Python:


from collections import deque


def euler(v, graph, visited):
    print(v)
    for u in graph.get(v, list()):
        if not visited[v][u]:
            visited[v][u] = True
            visited[u][v] = True
            euler(u, graph, visited)


def euler_no_recursion(v, graph, visited):
    stack = deque()
    stack.append(v)
    while stack:
        u = stack.pop()
        print(u)
        for w in reversed(graph.get(u, list())):
            if not visited[u][w]:
                visited[u][w] = True
                visited[w][u] = True
                stack.append(w)
 ^29i9dkSs

Код на C++:


#include <vector>
#include <stack>
#include <iostream>

void euler(int v, const std::vector<std::vector<int>> &graph, std::vector<std::vector<bool>> &visited) {
    std::cout << v << std::endl;
    for (int u: graph[v]) {
        if (not visited[v][u]) {
            visited[v][u] = true;
            visited[u][v] = true;
            euler(u, graph, visited);
        }
    }
}

void euler_no_recursion(int v, const std::vector<std::vector<int>> &graph, std::vector<std::vector<bool>> &visited) {
    std::stack<int> stack;
    stack.push(v);
    while (not stack.empty()) {
        int u = stack.top();
        stack.pop();
        std::cout << u << std::endl;
        for (auto it = graph[u].rbegin(); it != graph[u].rend(); ++it) {
            auto w = *it;
            if (not visited[u][w]) {
                visited[u][w] = true;
                visited[w][u] = true;
                stack.push(w);
            }
        }
    }
} ^NSUJt65G
